Infusion asc Stone Grey Perfect Fit (Blinds By Post)

Infusion asc stone grey perfect fit pleated blind. Part of their infusion asc range, where advanced solar control (asc) creates a perfect solution for any room, reducing the sun's glare whilst also increasing your energy efficiency. The asc refers to a reflective backing on the material which helps improve the energy efficiency of the blind by reflecting the heat out in the summer and retaining heat in the winter. The metallic reflective backing is therefore on the reverse of the fabric, facing towards the window. This fabric will still allow light into the room, but giving full privacy when inside from outside. This perfect fit blind is produced in a single cell fabric and can be mounted in a 'no drill, no screws' fitting to most double glazed, internally beaded, upvc windows and doors. The blind is fixed by brackets which sit between the black rubber bead and the glass, they simply slide in when installing - taking minutes per blind to fit and keeping the window guarantee! This is a single-cell fabric, the guide wires will be exposed meaning that there will be visible holes allowing light to come through. These can be seen on their range of images above. If you would prefer the wires to be hidden, please take a look at their 'hive' or 'luna' ranges. Made to measure infusion asc stone grey perfect fit pleated blind px4137. Their infusion range allows in natural light but has the added benefit of having an advanced solar coating which improves energy efficiency

This perfect fit blind is produced in a single cell fabric and can be mounted in a 'no drill, no screws' fitting to most double glazed, internally beaded, upvc windows and doors. The blind is fixed by brackets which sit between the black rubber bead and the glass, they simply slide in when installing - taking minutes per blind to fit and keeping the window guarantee! Infusion asc Saffron Perfect Fit (Blinds By Post)

Infusion asc saffron perfect fit pleated blind. Part of their infusion asc range, where advanced solar control (asc) creates a perfect solution for any room, reducing the sun's glare whilst also increasing your energy efficiency. The asc refers to a reflective backing on the material which helps improve the energy efficiency of the blind by reflecting the heat out in the summer and retaining heat in the winter. The metallic reflective backing is therefore on the reverse of the fabric, facing towards the window. This fabric will still allow light into the room, but giving full privacy when inside from outside. This perfect fit blind is produced in a single cell fabric and can be mounted in a 'no drill, no screws' fitting to most double glazed, internally beaded, upvc windows and doors. The blind is fixed by brackets which sit between the black rubber bead and the glass, they simply slide in when installing - taking minutes per blind to fit and keeping the window guarantee! This is a single-cell fabric, the guide wires will be exposed meaning that there will be visible holes allowing light to come through. These can be seen on their range of images above. If you would prefer the wires to be hidden, please take a look at their 'hive' or 'luna' ranges. Made to measure infusion asc saffron perfect fit pleated blind px4141. Their infusion range allows in natural light but has the added benefit of having an advanced solar coating which improves energy efficiency

If you're looking for energy efficient blinds, celluar pleated blinds are effective at keeping your house warm during the winter and cool during the summer. Featured here in their staple neutral ivory colour - they're both attractive and stylish additions to your room. This fabric is also a blackout fabric which allows you to fully control the light in your room. Hampton Grey Pleated Perfect Fit (Make My Blinds)

For a darker grey in your window the hampton grey pleated is a superb option. The colour is not created in a block but rather created from a series of short strokes of mid-tone and darker greys, which layer into a deep grey fabric. Additional shading comes from the pleated ripples that create natural highlights and pooling shadows. The perfect fit blind fits to the window frame itself as opposed to installing on the wall, for tools-free installation in under 15 minutes. Struggling to cover your french doors? Pleated perfect fit blinds are a great way to shade each pane, and provide style and privacy at the same time. The pleated fabric gently filters the light coming into your room, while still giving you peaceful seclusion. Looking for a solution for your conservatory windows? Perfect fits are designed to clip on quickly and easily - with no screws, drilling or tools required Hampton grey pleated perfect fit

Hampton Dove Pleated Perfect Fit (Make My Blinds)

Grey is the new white in the world of interiors, and this hampton dove is a particularly on-trend shade. Instead of a block colour, the polyester blind is made up of short strokes of lighter and darker greys, for a lively and organic effect. These horizontal strokes marry well with the pleated ripples that run throughout the fabric, the concertina effect creating its own natural highlights and pooling shadows.
